    <script nomodule="" src="https://assets.zephr.com/zephr-browser/1.5.1/zephr-browser.umd.js"></script>
    
    <script type="module">
      import * as zephrBrowser from 'https://assets.zephr.com/zephr-browser/1.5.1/zephr-browser.modern.js';
    
      // function to get the cookie content
      const getCookieContent = (cookie) => {
        const cookieContent = document.cookie.split(';').find(item => item.trim().startsWith(`${cookie}=`));
        if (!cookieContent) {
          return false;
        }
        const cookieValue = cookieContent.split(`${cookie}=`);
        if (!cookieValue[1]) {
          return false;
        }
        return cookieValue[1];
      };
    
      // on DOMContentLoaded
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', (event) => {
        // set the default payload for Zephr
        const payload = {
          customData : {
            "wallet-connected": false,
          }
        };
    
        // set the JWT token if present
        const identityToken = getCookieContent('TASLogin');
        if (identityToken) {
          payload.jwt = identityToken;
        }
    
        // set the status of wallet connect to true if the cooke is present
        if (getCookieContent('wallet_sub')) {
          payload.customData['wallet-connected'] = true;
        }
    
        // set the meter height
        const meterValue = getCookieContent('time_meter_v2');
        if (meterValue && meterValue.split('|')[0]) {
          payload.customData['meter-height'] = parseInt(meterValue.split('|')[0]);
        }
    
        // get the tags
        const articleTags = "homepage";
    
        // iterate through the tags and add it to the payload as key value
        if (articleTags) {
          const articleTagArray = articleTags.split(',');
          articleTagArray.forEach((element) => {
            payload.customData[`article-tag-${element}`] = true;
          });
        }
    
        if (debugMode) {
          console.log('zephr-payload', payload);
        }
    
        zephrBrowser.run(payload)
        .catch(error => {
          if (debugMode) {
            console.log(error, 'ZephrBrowser.run Error');
          }
        });
      });
    </script>

      const btnThree = document.getElementsByClassName(
        "campaign-three_close-button"
      );
      if (btnThree?.[0]) {
        btnThree[0].addEventListener("click", closeModal, false);

        function closeModal(event) {

    </script><script src="https://code.jquery.com/jquery-3.3.1.min.js"></script><script>
  const outcomeName = "standard_disengaged_offer";
  const timestampStorageName = outcomeName + "-storage-timestamp";
  const countStorageName = outcomeName + "-storage-count";
  const firstViewStorageName = outcomeName + "-first-view-timestamp";
  const appearedOnPage = "appeared-disengage";

  const timeOutSec = 60;
  const viewInHours = 12;
  const resetInDays = 30;
  const maxTimesView = 4;

  // Get the modal
  const modal_dis = document.getElementById("banner_image_bottom");

  let mouseX = 0;
  let mouseY = 0;
  let popupCounter = 0;

  function diff_hours(dt2, dt1) {
    var diff = (dt2 - dt1) / 1000;
    diff /= 60 * 60;
    return Math.abs(Math.round(diff));
  }

  function isRegwallHidden() {
    var regwalls = document.getElementsByClassName("registration-wall-wrapper");
    if (regwalls[0] == null) return true;
    else return regwalls[0].offsetParent === null;
  }

  var inactivityTime = function () {
    var time;
    // DOM Events
    document.addEventListener("mousemove", function (e) {
      mouseX = e.clientX;
      mouseY = e.clientY;
    });

    $(document).mouseleave(function () {
      if (mouseY < 100 && popupCounter == 0) {
        showOverlay(true);
        popupCounter++;
      }
    });

    resetTimer();
    document.onmousemove = resetTimer;
    document.onmousedown = resetTimer; // touchscreen presses
    document.ontouchstart = resetTimer;
    document.onclick = resetTimer; // touchpad clicks
    document.onkeydown = resetTimer; // onkeypress is deprectaed
    document.addEventListener("scroll", resetTimer, true);

    function showOverlay(intent) {
      const recordCount = localStorage.getItem(countStorageName);
      const recordTimestamp = localStorage.getItem(timestampStorageName);
      const entranceOverlayDisplayed = localStorage.getItem(
        "entranceOverlayDisplayed"
      );
      const gdprModalCheck = document.getElementById("onetrust-banner-sdk");
      if (
        (!gdprModalCheck || gdprModalCheck?.style.display === "none") && (
          !entranceOverlayDisplayed || entranceOverlayDisplayed === "false"
        ) &&
        isRegwallHidden() &&
        ((!recordCount && !recordTimestamp) ||
          (recordCount &&
            recordTimestamp &&
            Number(recordCount) < Number(maxTimesView) &&
            diff_hours(recordTimestamp, new Date().getTime()) >
              Number(viewInHours)))
      ) {
        localStorage.setItem(appearedOnPage, "true");
        localStorage.setItem(
          countStorageName,
          !recordCount && !recordTimestamp ? 1 : Number(recordCount) + 1
        );
        localStorage.setItem(timestampStorageName, new Date().getTime());
        if (!recordCount) {
          localStorage.setItem(firstViewStorageName, new Date().getTime());
        }
        window?.dataLayer?.push({
          event: "user_behavior",
          outcome: outcomeName,
          action: !!intent
            ? "disengage_with_intent"
            : "disengage_with_inactivity",
        });
        modal_dis.style.display = "block";
      }
    }

    function resetTimer() {
      clearTimeout(time);
      time = setTimeout(showOverlay, Number(timeOutSec) * 1000);
    }
  };

  window.onload = function () {
    localStorage.setItem(appearedOnPage, "false");
    const firstViewTimestamp = localStorage.getItem(firstViewStorageName);
    if (
      firstViewTimestamp &&
      diff_hours(firstViewTimestamp, new Date().getTime()) > resetInDays * 24
    ) {
      localStorage.setItem(firstViewStorageName, new Date().getTime());
      localStorage.removeItem(timestampStorageName);
      localStorage.removeItem(countStorageName);
    }
    inactivityTime();
  };
</script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://use.typekit.net/nga7gkm.css/"><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://use.typekit.net/ulq1cul.css"><style>

      const btnFour = document.getElementsByClassName(
        "campaign-four_close-button"
      );
      if (btnFour?.[0]) {
        btnFour[0].addEventListener("click", closeModal, false);

        function closeModal(event) {
          event.preventDefault();
          document.getElementById("banner_timer").style.display = "none";
        }
      }

      let timerDuration = "5";
      function startTimer(duration, display) {
        var timer = duration,
          minutes,
          seconds;
        setInterval(function () {
          minutes = parseInt(timer / 60, 10);
          seconds = parseInt(timer % 60, 10);

          minutes = minutes < 10 ? "0" + minutes : minutes;
          seconds = seconds < 10 ? "0" + seconds : seconds;

          display.innerHTML = minutes + ":" + seconds;

          if (--timer < 0) {
            timer = duration;
          }
        }, 1000);
      }

      const minutes = parseInt(timerDuration) * 60;
      const component = document.getElementById("countdown-timer");
      startTimer(minutes, component);
    </script><script>
  var entranceTimeOutSec = 2;
  const delayForVideoInSeconds = 15;
  var videoClass = document.getElementsByClassName("lead-video");
  const appearedOnPageStoreName = "appeared-disengage";
  const appearedOnPageValue = localStorage.getItem(appearedOnPageStoreName);
  const outcomeNameEntrance = "standard_entrance";

  if (videoClass[0] != null) {
    entranceTimeOutSec = 15;
  }

  function showEntranceModal() {
    const modal = document.getElementById("banner_timer");
    if (
      isRegwallHidden() &&
      (!appearedOnPageValue || appearedOnPageValue === "false")
    ) {
      localStorage.setItem("entranceOverlayDisplayed", "true");

      setTimeout(function () {
        window?.dataLayer?.push({
          event: "user_behavior",
          outcome: outcomeNameEntrance,
          action:
            entranceTimeOutSec === delayForVideoInSeconds
              ? "entrance_delay_for_video"
              : "entrance_no_delay",
        });
        modal.style.display = "block";
      }, entranceTimeOutSec * 1000);
    } else {
      localStorage.setItem("entranceOverlayDisplayed", "false");
      modal.style.display = "none";
    }
  }

  function isRegwallHidden() {
    var regwalls = document.getElementsByClassName("registration-wall-wrapper");
    if (regwalls[0] == null) return true;
    else return regwalls[0].offsetParent === null;
  }

  setTimeout(function () {
    const gdprModal = document.getElementById("onetrust-banner-sdk");

    if (gdprModal) {
      var observer = new MutationObserver(function (mutationsList, observer) {
        for (var mutation of mutationsList) {
          if (gdprModal.style.display == "none") {
            showEntranceModal();
          }
        }
      });
      observer.observe(document.getElementById("onetrust-banner-sdk"), {
        attributes: true,
      });
    } else {
      showEntranceModal();
    }
  }, 3000);

      <div class="partial video-section">
        <div class="video-inner">
          <a href="/collection/video/">
            <h2 class="section-heading video-section__heading">Video<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" role="img" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"><polygon points="10 6 8.59 7.41 13.17 12 8.59 16.59 10 18 16 12"></polygon></svg></h2>
          </a>
          <div class="component homepage-video-player">
            <div class="player">
                <div class="video-container" data-media-id="eqrZmIir">
          <div class="partial aspect-ratio-box" style="--aspect-ratio:1.7777777777777777; --mobile-aspect-ratio:1.7777777777777777;">
                      <div id="jw--e0fe3bab-d54f-4eb3-b80e-1c78d8302399" class="jwplayer jw-reset jw-state-setup jw-stretch-uniform jw-flag-aspect-mode" tabindex="0" aria-label="Video Player" role="application" style="width: 100%;"><div class="jw-aspect jw-reset" style="padding-top: 56.25%;"></div><div class="jw-wrapper jw-reset"><div class="jw-top jw-reset"></div><div class="jw-aspect jw-reset" style="padding-top: 56.25%;"></div><div class="jw-media jw-reset"></div><div class="jw-preview jw-reset"></div><div class="jw-captions jw-reset"><div class="jw-captions-window jw-reset"><span class="jw-captions-text jw-reset"></span></div></div><div class="jw-title jw-reset-text" dir="auto"><div class="jw-title-primary jw-reset-text"></div><div class="jw-title-secondary jw-reset-text"></div></div><div class="jw-overlays jw-reset"></div><div class="jw-hidden-accessibility"><span class="jw-time-update" aria-live="assertive"></span><span class="jw-volume-update" aria-live="assertive"></span></div></div><div class="afs_ads ad-placement" style="width: 1px; height: 1px; position: absolute; background: transparent;">&nbsp;</div></div>

                <div class="video-info">
                  <div class="info-left">
                    <h3 class="title">Paramore Revisits Its Expansive Discography, From All We Know Is Falling to This Is Why</h3>
                    <span class="date-and-duration">Feb 6, 2023<span class="divider">|</span>9:44</span>
                  </div>
                  <div class="info-right">
                    <p class="description">When Paramore first formed, it was composed of brothers Josh and Zac Farro, who played guitar and drums, respectively, lead singer Hayley Williams, bassist Jeremy Davis, and guitarist Jason Bynum. But over the last 20 years, the band has evolved into its current and arguably best iteration: Williams, Zac Farro, and guitarist Taylor York. </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
            </div>
